var theForm = document.forms['aspnetForm'];

if (!theForm) {

    theForm = document.aspnetForm;

}

function __doPostBack(eventTarget, eventArgument) {

    if (!theForm.onsubmit || (theForm.onsubmit() != false)) {

        theForm.__EVENTTARGET.value = eventTarget;

        theForm.__EVENTARGUMENT.value = eventArgument;

        theForm.submit();

    }

}

     overview.InitDone = false;

function overview_ApplyChanges(response) {

    for (var i = 0; i < response.length; i++) {

        var value = response[i].Value;

        if (response[i].ParameterType == "boolean")

            value = (value.toLowerCase() == "true");

 try {

         if(response[i].ParameterType == "string[]" || response[i].ParameterType == "integer[]") 

         overview[response[i].ParameterId](response[i].Values);

         else

         overview[response[i].ParameterId](value);

 }catch(e){}

    }

}

   <script language="javascript">

function ExpandingButtons_Init() {

	if ( !ExpandingButtons_BrowserCapable() ) { return; }

		

	for( var i=0; i<ComitIrl_Common_Controls_Web_ExpandingButtons.length; i++ ) {

		var expandingButtonDeclaration = ComitIrl_Common_Controls_Web_ExpandingButtons[i].split(";");

		if ( expandingButtonDeclaration.length != 6 ) { return; }

		

		var expanderControl = document.getElementById( expandingButtonDeclaration[0] );

		var targetControl = document.getElementById( expandingButtonDeclaration[1] );

		var trackerControl = document.getElementById( expandingButtonDeclaration[2] );

		var expandedValue = expandingButtonDeclaration[3];

		var contractedValue = expandingButtonDeclaration[4];

		var valueChanger = expandingButtonDeclaration[5];

		

		if ( expanderControl != null && targetControl != null && trackerControl != null ) {

			expanderControl.TargetControl = expandingButtonDeclaration[1];

			expanderControl.TrackerControl = expandingButtonDeclaration[2];

			expanderControl.ToggleView = ExpandingButtons_Toggle;

			expanderControl.onclick = expanderControl.ToggleView;

			expanderControl.ExpandedValue = expandedValue;

			expanderControl.ContractedValue = contractedValue;

			switch( valueChanger ) {

				case "b":

					expanderControl.ToggleValue = ExpandingButtons_ToggleButtonText;

					break;

				case "l":

					expanderControl.ToggleValue = ExpandingButtons_ToggleLinkText;

					break;

				case "i":

					expanderControl.ToggleValue = ExpandingButtons_ToggleImageSrc;

					break;

			}

		} else {

			alert("ComitIrl.Common.Controls.Web ExpandingButtons has a problem. Please check the page configuration.");

		}

	}

}

function ExpandingButtons_BrowserCapable() {

	if ( typeof( document.getElementById ) == "undefined" ) {

		return false;

	}

	return true;

}

//PC1971 changed ExpandingButtons_Toggle function below to implement 'Collaspe All' and 'Expand all Sections' image buttons

//This is done in EO_BuildDetails.aspx and EO_BuildDetails.js?v=200610

//Existing behaviour to other page should remain unchanged



var expClpsAllAction = ''; 

function ExpandingButtons_Toggle(event) {

	if ( typeof( window.event ) != "undefined" && typeof( window.event.returnValue ) != "undefined" ) {

		window.event.returnValue = false;

	}

  var targetcontrol = document.getElementById(this.TargetControl);

  var trackerControl = document.getElementById(this.TrackerControl);

  if(expClpsAllAction=='')

  {

	  if ( targetcontrol.style.display == "none" ) {

		  targetcontrol.style.display = "";

		  trackerControl.value = "True";

		  this.ToggleValue(this.ExpandedValue);

		  return false;

	  } else {

		  targetcontrol.style.display = "none";

		  trackerControl.value = "False";

		  this.ToggleValue(this.ContractedValue);

		  return false;

	  }

  }else

  {

 		  targetcontrol.style.display = expClpsAllAction=="expand"?"":"none";

		  trackerControl.value = expClpsAllAction=="expand"?"True":"False";

		  this.ToggleValue( expClpsAllAction=="expand"?this.ExpandedValue:this.ContractedValue);

		  return false;

  }

	return false;

}

function ExpandingButtons_ToggleButtonText(newValue) {

	this.value = newValue;

}

function ExpandingButtons_ToggleLinkText(newValue) {

	this.innerText = newValue;

}

function ExpandingButtons_ToggleImageSrc(newValue) {

	var newValues = newValue.split("__");

	this.alt = newValues[0];

	this.src = newValues[1];

}

<!--

	var ListLinkManager = new Object();

	

	//Bug X08_0256 - Problem with webservice translation not working for startup script.  If statement put in for the case

	//where this variable has not been declared in the pagetemplate code.

	if (typeof(gsNoneOption) != "undefined")

	{

		ListLinkManager["empty"] = new Array("", gsNoneOption);

	}

	else

	{

		ListLinkManager["empty"] = new Array("", getTran("-- None --"));

	}

		

	function ListLink_Init() {

		for( var i = 0; i < ListLinks.length; i++ ) {

			var listRelation = ListLinks[i].split(";");

			if ( listRelation.length != 2 ) { return; }

			var parentControl = ListLink_FindList( listRelation[0] );

			var childControl = ListLink_FindList( listRelation[1] );

			if ( parentControl != null  ) {

				ListLink_Load( parentControl, childControl );

			}

		}

	}

	function ListLink_Load( parent, child ) {

	

		if (!parent.ChildLists) {

			parent.ChildLists = new Array();

		}

		parent.ChildLists[parent.ChildLists.length] = child;

		parent.RepopulateChildren = ListLink_RepopulateChildren;

		parent.GetParentValueKey = ListLink_GetParentValueKey;

		parent.onchange = function(e) { this.RepopulateChildren(); $(child).trigger("liszt:updated"); };

	}

	

	function ListLink_SetDefaults() {

		//alert ('In ListLink_SetDefaults');

		for( var i = 0; i < ListLinks.length; i++ ) {

			var listRelation = ListLinks[i].split(";");

			if ( listRelation.length != 2 ) { return; }

			var parentControl = ListLink_FindList( listRelation[0] );

			if ( parentControl != null ) {

				parentControl.RepopulateChildren();

			}

		}

	}

	function ListLink_FindList( name ) {

		for( var i = 0; i < document.forms.length; i++ ) {

			var theForm = document.forms[i];

			var theList = theForm[name];

			if ( theList != null ) {

				return theList;

			}

		}

		return null;

	}

	function ListLink_RepopulateChildren() 

	{	

		if (this.ChildLists)

		{

			for ( var i = 0; i < this.ChildLists.length; i++ ) 

			{			

				if (this.ChildLists[i])

				{

					ListLink_ClearList(this.ChildLists[i]);

					ListLink_FillList(this.ChildLists[i], this.GetParentValueKey(this.ChildLists[i]));

				}

			}

		}

	}

	function ListLink_ClearList(list){

		if ( list.ChildLists ) {

			for( var j = 0; j < list.ChildLists.length; j++ ) 

			{	

				if (list.ChildLists[j])

				{

					ListLink_ClearList( list.ChildLists[j] );

				}

			}

		}

		if ( list.selectedIndex >= 0 ) {

			list.originalSelectedValue = list.options[list.selectedIndex].value;

		} else {

			list.originalSelectedValue = "";

		}

		var lastIndex = list.options.length - 1;

		for (var i = lastIndex; i >= 0; i--){

			list.options[i] = null;

		}

		list.selectedIndex = -1;

	}

	function ListLink_GetParentValueKey(childList) {

		if ( this.selectedIndex != -1 ) {

			return this.name + "," + childList.name + "=" + this.options[this.selectedIndex].value;

		} else {

			return "";

		}

	}

	function ListLink_FillList(list, parentValue){

		var emptyItem = ListLinkManager["empty"];

		list.options[0] = new Option(emptyItem[1], emptyItem[0]);

		if (parentValue != "" && ListLinkManager[parentValue]){

			var newChildItems = ListLinkManager[parentValue];

			if ( newChildItems.length > 0 ) {

				for (var i = 0; i < newChildItems.length; i = i + 2){

					list.options[list.options.length] = new Option(newChildItems[i + 1], newChildItems[i]);

					if ( list.options[list.options.length-1].value == list.originalSelectedValue ) {

						list.options[list.options.length-1].selected = true;

					}

				}

			}

		}

		if ( list.ChildLists ) {

			for ( var j = 0; j < list.ChildLists.length; j++ ) 

			{

				if (list.ChildLists[j])

				{

					ListLink_FillList(list.ChildLists[j], list.GetParentValueKey(list.ChildLists[j]));

				}

			}

		}

	}

//-->

</script>

function reason_ApplyChanges(response) {

    for (var i = 0; i < response.length; i++) {

        var value = response[i].Value;

        if (response[i].ParameterType == "boolean")

            value = (value.toLowerCase() == "true");

 try {

         if(response[i].ParameterType == "string[]" || response[i].ParameterType == "integer[]") 

         reason[response[i].ParameterId](response[i].Values);

         else

         reason[response[i].ParameterId](value);

 }catch(e){}

    }

}

 }catch(e){}

    }

                         </div><textarea name="ctl00$ctl00$content$content$ctl02$rtbLossDesc$tbRTF" rows="2" cols="20" id="ctl00_ctl00_content_content_ctl02_rtbLossDesc_tbRTF" class="READONLY" spellcheck="true" style="height: 85px; width: 700px; visibility: hidden; display: none;" data-ays-ignore="true" aria-hidden="true">On 15MAR2022, PASE received a payment request for $420,000.00 through internet banking profile of the client Zara Mining. In line with established process for all payments above $100,000.00, we requested that the customer furnish us with a copy of the invoice covering the transaction.&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;The customer in response to our request informed us that they did not initiate the payment. Our checks shows that the payment was initiated using one of the profiles created for the customer on internet banking. Whilst investigating the payment for $420,000.00 we noticed that another payment of $75,000.00 came through for the same customer.&lt;br&gt;We have suspended the profile of the customer in internet banking. We had a call with INTE and Infosys. We detected that some default setting for user creation on the e-banking platform was not set up as required.&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;These settings have to do with whether a one-time password is required for sign-on or not, which was set as blank in the case of the customer. Similar settings for other customers were extracted from the system and appropriately updated. Also, setting requesting for users of the platform to authorize transactions without rules were updated to NO to ensure that the workflow setup processes transactions by users&lt;br&gt;&lt;br&gt;All platform users going forward will require maker checker rules in place, and no single user may initiate and complete transactions.</textarea>
